Oakland Floats is quiet and peaceful, and Hannah answered every question about floating I didn't know I had, telling me tips and tricks to ensure I had a good time--put Vaseline on any small cuts on your fingers; be careful not to get the salt water in your eyes; if you do get salt in your eyes, use this solution; even different float techniques that people use! < Review>
My first floating experience was lovely. I wasn't sure what to expect and I was a little scared of the concept of a float tank but really curious so I went for it and im so happy I did.

The staff was really friendly and the atmosphere feels very private and calm. Upon arrival they offer you tea and water and once its ready, they show you to your room. They ask you to take a shower before your float and then you can descend into the shallow depth of the float tank. From there on you just have to let the water do the work for you. It is so relaxing and healing. You just melt and let everything go. It is the best place to meditate and just plain relax. The water temperature is perfect and there are no distractions.

You will get the best nights sleep after a float here. I plan on making this a regular part of my self care regimen.

Highly recommend.<//Review>

< Review>
My boyfriend and I stumbled upon this place while we were at an outlet mall. We originally came to the mall to visit Zales and walked into Kevin's to price compare.

Kevin's ended up having the exact ring my boyfriend wanted so we decided to go ahead and purchase it. I got my ring as well. Prices seemed consistent with other stores and we liked the lifetime warranty that comes with purchasing from a well known store (though I had never heard of them until now).

The only issue we had was the salesperson quoted us a price that included the lifetime warranty and then when after they ran our card, we saw they had charged us extra $99 for it. I don't know if it was a communication issue or a salesperson deception. We think the latter. That is the reason for only 3 stars.

Once our rings arrive I may update this review. Fingers crossed there are no issues. They are supposed to be having them sent to a store closer to us. Mine will take a couple days and his up to a month since they have to special order his size 14. All in all we are happy to have our rings and move on to honeymoon planning.</Review>
